FNV PPLIGHTING TEXTURE RUNTIME BINDING FOLLOWUP AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which vtable/class variants use BSShaderPPLighting::SetupGeometry at 0x00BDF790?
2. Where is shader object field +0xDC written, cleared, or addrefed in renderer code?
3. Does +0xDC point to a texture set, shader property, or some other material resource?
4. How do source texture-set slots from FUN_00877A30 reach draw-time shader texture stages?
